riscv64-unknown-linux-gnu-gcc -march=rv32ima -mabi=ilp32 -O0 -g -c asm/start.S -o asm/start.o

xargo build --features qemu --target=riscv32imac-unknown-none-elf

qemu-system-riscv32 -machine sifive_e -nographic -serial mon:stdio -kernel mosin_os.elf
